<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:notie.html>notie</a> (33179)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:notie.html>notie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:noties.html>noties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:notie.html>notietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a> (96)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a></i>, a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>now; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i></span></span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a>?</i>
<dl><dd>What <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> it <b>now</b>?</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>come on; <span class="use-with-mention">modal particle indicating a certain degree of urgency or impatience on behalf of the speaker.</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>Ga</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a></b>! <a href = vnd.unilang:straks.html>Straks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>kom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a>!</i>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>so, well; <span class="use-with-mention">when pressing someone</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>Nou</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vertel.html>vertel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarheid.html>waarheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a>!</i></dd>

<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>Nou</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waait.html>waait</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> hard <a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a>!</i>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nous.html>nous</a> (51137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νοῦς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">noûs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νόος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nóos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nous.html>nous</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">philosophy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The mind or intellect, reason, both rational and emotional
<ul><li><b>1900</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gilbert.html>Gilbert</a> Keith Chesterton, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/On_the_Disastrous_Spread_of_Aestheticism_in_all_Classes" class="extiw" title="s:On the Disastrous Spread of Aestheticism in all Classes">On the Disastrous Spread of Aestheticism in all Classes</a></i>
<dl><dd>I feel the will to roam, to learn</dd>
<dd>By test, experience, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nous.html>nous</a></b>,</dd>
<dd>That fire <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> hot and ocean deep,</dd>
<dd>And <a href = vnd.unilang:wolves.html>wolves</a> carnivorous.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>In Neoplatonism, the divine reason, regarded as first divine emanation.</li>
<li>Common sense; practical intelligence.</li></ol>

***nouvelle.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nouvelle.html>nouvelle</a> (90139)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Non-lemma form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:nouvelle.html>nouvelle</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">feminine singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:nouveau.html>nouveau</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">new</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">Jérôme a acheté sa <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nouvelle.html>nouvelle</a></b> voiture <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Jerome bought his <b>new</b> car yesterday.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:nouvelle.html>nouvelle</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">novele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*novella</i>, substantivized neuter plural form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">novellus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">new, novel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">novella</i>.
</p><p>Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:novelle.html>novelle</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:nouvelle.html>nouvelle</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fr p-form-of" lang="fr">nouvelles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>news, a piece of information
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">J'ai appris la <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nouvelle.html>nouvelle</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:soir.html>soir</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> the <b>news</b> yesterday evening.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>novella</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:novelle.html>novelle</a> (37965)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:nouvelle.html>nouvelle</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:novelle.html>novelle</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:novelles.html>novelles</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">novellen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:novelle.html>novelletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a literary essay on closely related events</li>
<li>a short novel, short story</li></ol>

***nox.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> nox (18503)</h1><br></body> 
***nozem.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nozem.html>nozem</a> (40441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>About 1920, from the Bargoens cant. Probably borrowed from Yiddish. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nozem.html>nozem</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nozems.html>nozems</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nozempje.html>nozempje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>someone who belonged to a 1950s Dutch youth culture revolving around (light) motorcycles, similar to a <span class="Latn" lang="en">greaser</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">raggare</span> or <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:teddy.html>Teddy</a> boy</span></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:rowdy.html>rowdy</a>, especially one with long hair, beard and <a href = vnd.unilang:tattoos.html>tattoos</a> like an archetypical <a href = vnd.unilang:hells.html>Hells</a> Angel</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:cultuur.html>cultuur</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfbewust.html>zelfbewuste</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:stoer.html>stoer</a> geklede, <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> vetkuif <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> buikschuiver <a href = vnd.unilang:voorzien.html>voorziene</a>  branieschopper (<a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaren.html>jaren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijftig.html>vijftig</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:zestig.html>zestig</a>)</li>

</p>
<ol><li>prosaic, matter of fact</li>
<li>sober, not drunk</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a person</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> having neither eaten nor drunk anything</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a body</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> empty as a result of fasting</li>

***nummer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nummer.html>nummer</a> (469)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nommer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">nombre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">numerus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nummer.html>nummer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nummers.html>nummers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nummertje.html>nummertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>number used as a means of identification</li>
<li>number (used to show the rank of something in a list or sequence)</li>
<li>a song or musical performance; a track</li>
<li>issue of a publication (e.g. a magazine)</li>
<li>number of an item on a menu; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a dish identified by such a number</li></ol>

***nummerbord.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nummerbord.html>nummerbord</a> (14214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nummer.html>nummer</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bord.html>bord</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">nytt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">use, <a href = vnd.unilang:utility.html>utility</a>, advantage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">use</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nutteloosheid.html>nutteloosheid</a> (102331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nutteloos.html>nutteloos</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nutteloosheid.html>nutteloosheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nutteloosheid.html>nutteloosheden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nutteloosheid.html>nutteloosheidje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***nuttig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nuttig.html>nuttig</a> (4150)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:nutte.html>nutte</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">useful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nutiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">useful, useable, profitable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*neutaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*newd-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize; grasp; use</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>

<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nutteloos.html>nutteloos</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onbruikbaar.html>onbruikbaar</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
